AS-02 REST API API documentation version 0.1

http://{server}/{api}/

AMWA AS-02 RESTful API

The AS-02 RESTful API provides a means to manage a collection of AS-02 bundles as they change and grow, whilst hiding some of the details of the underlying implementation, e.g. file system or MXF files. The API is expected to be associated with a specific store, such as a folder on a file system or a bucket of objects on an object store.

Bundle Collection

Provides access to all bundles stored in this collection.

/bundle get post

get

Retrieve a paged list of all stored bundles.

post

Create a new empty bundle. An empty bundle is a bundle with an empty media folder and an empty extra folder.

The bundle must have a unique identifier (BundleID) and name (BundleName) on this store. The creation date (CreationDate) property for the bundle will be automatically set to current system time. Annotations (AnnotationText) in the bundle will be an initially empty list.

get /bundle

Retrieve a paged list of all stored bundles.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • skip: (integer)

    Number of pages of bundle items to skip (hide) before starting to display values.

  • limit: (integer - default: 20)

    Limit of the mixumum number of bundle items to include on each page.

  • detail: (one of full, summary, link - default: full)

    Amount of detail to return for each bundle items in the collection, where:

    • full: Complete manifest details for each item.
    • summary: Some useful details about each bundle, including its name, identifier, creator and number of files.
    • link: A list of identifiers for bundles.

HTTP status code 200

Lists all stored bundles subject to the paging constraints.

Body

Type: application/xml

Schema:

<xs:schema attributeFormDefault="unqualified"
       elementFormDefault="qualified"
       xmlns:xs="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema"
       xmlns:as02="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/manifest"
       xmlns:atom="http://www.w3.org/2005/Atom"
       targetNamespace="http://www.quantel.com/qstack/rasotwo">
  <import namespace="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/manifest/" schemaLocation="AS-02Manifest.xsd"/>
  <xs:element name="Bundles">
    <xs:complexType>
      <xs:choice>
        <xs:element ref="as02:Manifest" minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"/> <!-- for full listings-->
        <xs:element name="BundleSummary" minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"> <!-- for summary listings -->
          <xs:complexType>
            <xs:sequence>
              <xs:element name="BundleName" minOccurs="1" maxOccurs="1" type="xs:string"/> 
              <xs:element name="BundleID" minOccurs="1" maxOccurs="1" type="as02:UUID"/>
              <xs:element name="FileCount" minOccurs="1" maxOccuts="1" type="xs:integer"/>
             </xs:sequence>
          </xs:complexType>
        </xs:element>
        <xs:element ref="atom:link" minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"/> <!-- for link only listings-->
      <xs:choice>
    </xs:complexType>
  </xs:element>
</xs:schema>

post /bundle

Create a new empty bundle. An empty bundle is a bundle with an empty media folder and an empty extra folder.

The bundle must have a unique identifier (BundleID) and name (BundleName) on this store. The creation date (CreationDate) property for the bundle will be automatically set to current system time. Annotations (AnnotationText) in the bundle will be an initially empty list.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • id: (string - pattern: (urn:uuid:)?[0-9a-fA-f]{8}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{12})

    An unique identifier for a new resource provided prior to its creation. The service will either:

    • proceed to try to create a resource with the given identifier, or
    • respond with a bad request status.

    This is an optional parameter of type UUID. If no id is provided, the service will generate a type 4 pseudo-random UUID to identify the resource.

  • name: (string)

    A unique name for this bundle on this store. If no name is provided, one will be automatically generated. The name is stored in the bundle's manifest file as element BundleName.

  • creator: (string)

    Bundle creator property, stored in Creator property of the bundle manifest file. If no creator is provided, a name for the local service may be used.

HTTP status code 201

Successful creation of a new bundle.

Headers

  • Location: (string)

    Full URL path to the newly created bundle, which includes the bundle ID.

Body

Type: application/xml

Schema:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<xs:schema xmlns:xs="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema"
    xmlns:mft="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/manifest"
    targetNamespace="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/manifest"
    elementFormDefault="qualified"
    attributeFormDefault="unqualified">
    <!-- ManifestType -->
    <xs:complexType name="ManifestType">
        <xs:sequence>
            <xs:element name="BundleName" type="xs:string"/>
            <xs:element name="BundleID" type="mft:UUID"/>
            <xs:element name="Creator" type="xs:string"/>
            <xs:element name="CreationDate" type="xs:dateTime"/>
            <xs:element name="AnnotationText" type="xs:string" minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"/>
            <xs:element name="FileList">
                <xs:complexType>
                    <xs:sequence>
                        <xs:element name="File" type="mft:FileType" maxOccurs="unbounded"/>
                    </xs:sequence>
                </xs:complexType>
            </xs:element>
            <xs:any minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded" namespace="##other" processContents="lax"/>
        </xs:sequence>
        <xs:anyAttribute namespace="##other" processContents="lax"/>
    </xs:complexType>
    <!-- FileType -->
    <xs:complexType name="FileType">
        <xs:sequence>
            <xs:element name="FileID" type="mft:IdType"/>
            <xs:element name="Role" type="mft:FileRole"/>
            <xs:element name="Size" type="xs:nonNegativeInteger"/>
            <xs:element name="Path" type="xs:anyURI"/>
            <xs:element name="MIC" minOccurs="0">
                <xs:complexType>
                    <xs:simpleContent>
                        <xs:extension base="xs:hexBinary">
                            <xs:attribute name="type" type="mft:MICTypeType" use="required"/>
                            <xs:attribute name="scope" type="mft:MICScopeType" use="required"/>
                        </xs:extension>
                    </xs:simpleContent>
                </xs:complexType>
            </xs:element>
            <xs:element name="AnnotationText" type="xs:string" 
                minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"/>
            <xs:any minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded" namespace="##other"
                processContents="lax"/>
        </xs:sequence>
        <xs:anyAttribute namespace="##other" processContents="lax"/>
    </xs:complexType>
    <!-- IdType -->
    <xs:simpleType name="IdType">
        <xs:union memberTypes="mft:UUID mft:UMID mft:UL mft:emptyID"/>
    </xs:simpleType>    
    <!-- UUID -->
    <xs:simpleType name="UUID">
        <xs:restriction base="xs:string">
            <xs:pattern
                value="urn:uuid:[0-9a-fA-F]{8}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{12}"/>
        </xs:restriction>
    </xs:simpleType>
    <!-- UMID -->
    <xs:simpleType name="UMID">
        <xs:restriction base="xs:string">
            <xs:pattern value="urn:smpte:umid:([0-9a-fA-F]{8}\.){7}[0-9a-fA-F]{8}"/>
        </xs:restriction>
    </xs:simpleType>
    <!-- UL -->
    <xs:simpleType name="UL">
        <xs:restriction base="xs:string">
            <xs:pattern
                value="urn:smpte:ul:([0-9a-fA-F]{8}\.){3}[0-9a-fA-F]{8}"/>
        </xs:restriction>
    </xs:simpleType>
	<xs:simpleType name="emptyID">
		<xs:restriction base="xs:string">
			<xs:pattern value=""/>
		</xs:restriction>
	</xs:simpleType>
    <!-- MICTypeType -->
    <xs:simpleType name="MICTypeType">
        <xs:restriction base="xs:string">
           <xs:enumeration value="hmac-sha1"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="crc32"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="crc16"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="md5"/>
        </xs:restriction>
    </xs:simpleType>
    <!-- MICScopeType -->
    <xs:simpleType name="MICScopeType">
        <xs:restriction base="xs:string">
            <xs:enumeration value="essence_only"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="entire_file"/>
        </xs:restriction>
    </xs:simpleType>
    <!-- FileRole -->
    <xs:simpleType name="FileRole">
        <xs:restriction base="xs:string">
            <xs:enumeration value="file"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="version"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="essencecomponent"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="shim"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="manifest"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="qc"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="graphic"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="caption"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="folder"/>
        </xs:restriction>
    </xs:simpleType>
    <xs:element name="Manifest" type="mft:ManifestType"/>
</xs:schema>

HTTP status code 400

Problem with the given parameters. Bundle could not be created.

Body

Type: application/xml

Schema:

     elementFormDefault="qualified"
     xmlns:xs="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema"
     targetNamespace="http://www.quantel.com/qstack/rasotwo">
  <xs:element name="error">
    <xs:complexType>
      <xs:sequence>
        <xs:element name="statusCode" type="xs:integer"/>
        <xs:element name="statusCodeMeaning" type="xs:string"/>
        <xs:element name="message" type="xs:string"/>
      </xs:sequence>
    </xs:complexType>
  </xs:element>
</xs:schema>

/bundle/{bundleID} get delete post

Create, read and update a specific bundle and its sub-resources.

get

Retrieves the stored manifest describing bundleID.

delete

Delete the specified bundle. The bundle will no longer appear in the list of bundles.

post

Update the bundle's details by changing the creator or adding an annotation.

Note that the update of the bundle's name is not supported because some bundle store implementations use the bundle name as a folder name on disk.

get /bundle/{bundleID}

Retrieves the stored manifest describing bundleID.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

HTTP status code 200

Bundle exists and current state of manifest file is provided.

Body

Type: application/xml

Schema:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<xs:schema xmlns:xs="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema"
    xmlns:mft="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/manifest"
    targetNamespace="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/manifest"
    elementFormDefault="qualified"
    attributeFormDefault="unqualified">
    <!-- ManifestType -->
    <xs:complexType name="ManifestType">
        <xs:sequence>
            <xs:element name="BundleName" type="xs:string"/>
            <xs:element name="BundleID" type="mft:UUID"/>

            <xs:element name="CreationDate" type="xs:dateTime"/>
            <xs:element name="AnnotationText" type="xs:string" minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"/>

    </xs:simpleType>

        <xs:restriction base="xs:string">
            <xs:pattern value="urn:smpte:umid:([0-9a-fA-F]{8}\.){7}[0-9a-fA-F]{8}"/>

    </xs:simpleType>
    <!-- UL -->
    <xs:simpleType name="UL">
        <xs:restriction base="xs:string">
            <xs:pattern
                value="urn:smpte:ul:([0-9a-fA-F]{8}\.){3}[0-9a-fA-F]{8}"/>
        </xs:restriction>
    </xs:simpleType>
	<xs:simpleType name="emptyID">
		<xs:restriction base="xs:string">
			<xs:pattern value=""/>
		</xs:restriction>
	</xs:simpleType>
    <!-- MICTypeType -->
    <xs:simpleType name="MICTypeType">
        <xs:restriction base="xs:string">
           <xs:enumeration value="hmac-sha1"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="crc32"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="crc16"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="md5"/>
        </xs:restriction>
    </xs:simpleType>
    <!-- MICScopeType -->
    <xs:simpleType name="MICScopeType">
        <xs:restriction base="xs:string">

delete /bundle/{bundleID}

Delete the specified bundle. The bundle will no longer appear in the list of bundles.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

HTTP status code 204

The bundle has been deleted successfully.

HTTP status code 404

The resource or one of its parent resources could not be found on this store.

post /bundle/{bundleID}

Update the bundle's details by changing the creator or adding an annotation.

Note that the update of the bundle's name is not supported because some bundle store implementations use the bundle name as a folder name on disk.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

Query Parameters

  • creator: (string)

    Bundle creator property, stored in Creator property of the bundle manifest file. If no creator is provided, the existing creator name will remain.

  • annotation: (string - repeat: true)

    List of annotations to add to the current annotations set for the bundle, stored as a sequence of AnnotationText elements in the bundle manifest file.

    This API does not support the editing or removal of annotations.

HTTP status code 200

Successful update of the properties provided with the updated manifest included in the response.

Body

Type: application/xml

Schema:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<xs:schema xmlns:xs="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema"
    xmlns:mft="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/manifest"
    targetNamespace="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/manifest"
    elementFormDefault="qualified"
    attributeFormDefault="unqualified">
    <!-- ManifestType -->
    <xs:complexType name="ManifestType">
        <xs:sequence>
            <xs:element name="BundleName" type="xs:string"/>
            <xs:element name="BundleID" type="mft:UUID"/>
            <xs:element name="Creator" type="xs:string"/>
            <xs:element name="CreationDate" type="xs:dateTime"/>
            <xs:element name="AnnotationText" type="xs:string" minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"/>
            <xs:element name="FileList">
                <xs:complexType>
                    <xs:sequence>
                        <xs:element name="File" type="mft:FileType" maxOccurs="unbounded"/>
                    </xs:sequence>
                </xs:complexType>
            </xs:element>
            <xs:any minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded" namespace="##other" processContents="lax"/>
        </xs:sequence>
        <xs:anyAttribute namespace="##other" processContents="lax"/>
    </xs:complexType>
    <!-- FileType -->
    <xs:complexType name="FileType">
        <xs:sequence>
            <xs:element name="FileID" type="mft:IdType"/>
            <xs:element name="Role" type="mft:FileRole"/>
            <xs:element name="Size" type="xs:nonNegativeInteger"/>
            <xs:element name="Path" type="xs:anyURI"/>
            <xs:element name="MIC" minOccurs="0">
                <xs:complexType>
                    <xs:simpleContent>
                        <xs:extension base="xs:hexBinary">
                            <xs:attribute name="type" type="mft:MICTypeType" use="required"/>
                            <xs:attribute name="scope" type="mft:MICScopeType" use="required"/>
                        </xs:extension>
                    </xs:simpleContent>
                </xs:complexType>
            </xs:element>
            <xs:element name="AnnotationText" type="xs:string" 
                minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"/>
            <xs:any minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded" namespace="##other"
                processContents="lax"/>
        </xs:sequence>
        <xs:anyAttribute namespace="##other" processContents="lax"/>
    </xs:complexType>
    <!-- IdType -->
    <xs:simpleType name="IdType">
        <xs:union memberTypes="mft:UUID mft:UMID mft:UL mft:emptyID"/>
    </xs:simpleType>    
    <!-- UUID -->
    <xs:simpleType name="UUID">
        <xs:restriction base="xs:string">
            <xs:pattern
                value="urn:uuid:[0-9a-fA-F]{8}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{12}"/>
        </xs:restriction>
    </xs:simpleType>
    <!-- UMID -->
    <xs:simpleType name="UMID">
        <xs:restriction base="xs:string">
            <xs:pattern value="urn:smpte:umid:([0-9a-fA-F]{8}\.){7}[0-9a-fA-F]{8}"/>
        </xs:restriction>
    </xs:simpleType>
    <!-- UL -->
    <xs:simpleType name="UL">
        <xs:restriction base="xs:string">
            <xs:pattern
                value="urn:smpte:ul:([0-9a-fA-F]{8}\.){3}[0-9a-fA-F]{8}"/>
        </xs:restriction>
    </xs:simpleType>
	<xs:simpleType name="emptyID">
		<xs:restriction base="xs:string">
			<xs:pattern value=""/>
		</xs:restriction>
	</xs:simpleType>
    <!-- MICTypeType -->
    <xs:simpleType name="MICTypeType">
        <xs:restriction base="xs:string">
           <xs:enumeration value="hmac-sha1"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="crc32"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="crc16"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="md5"/>
        </xs:restriction>
    </xs:simpleType>
    <!-- MICScopeType -->
    <xs:simpleType name="MICScopeType">
        <xs:restriction base="xs:string">
            <xs:enumeration value="essence_only"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="entire_file"/>
        </xs:restriction>
    </xs:simpleType>
    <!-- FileRole -->
    <xs:simpleType name="FileRole">
        <xs:restriction base="xs:string">
            <xs:enumeration value="file"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="version"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="essencecomponent"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="shim"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="manifest"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="qc"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="graphic"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="caption"/>
            <xs:enumeration value="folder"/>
        </xs:restriction>
    </xs:simpleType>
    <xs:element name="Manifest" type="mft:ManifestType"/>
</xs:schema>

/bundle/{bundleID}/media get post

Create, list, read, replace, grow and delete all essence component files (media files) in ths AS-02 bundle.

get

List details of all essence component files in the bundle.

post

Create a new empty essence component in the bundle using the given Reg-XML file descriptor. The essence component file will be open an ready for extension.

The body of the POST shall contain a valid Reg-XML (SMPTE 2001-2) serialization of a class that is the extension of an AAF FileDescriptor class.

  • For video data, this will be an extension of PictureDescriptor.
  • For audio data, this will be a SoundDescriptor or one of its extensions.
  • For ancilliary data, such as captions, this will an extension of DataEssenceDescriptor.

Certain properties of the descriptor will be used by the AS-02 API to determine aspects of theessence component to be created, such as index type (clip or frame wrapped), index edit rate etc..

get /bundle/{bundleID}/media

List details of all essence component files in the bundle.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

Query Parameters

  • skip: (integer)

    Number of pages of media items to skip (hide) before starting to display values.

  • limit: (integer - default: 20)

    Limit of the mixumum number of media items to include on each page.

  • detail: (one of full, summary, link - default: full)

    Amount of detail to return for each media items in the collection, where:

    • full: Complete manifest details for each item.
    • summary: Some useful details about each bundle, including its name, identifier, creator and number of files.
    • link: A list of identifiers for bundles.

HTTP status code 200

Successful retrieval of a list of file details.

Body

Type: application/xml

Schema:

<xs:schema attributeFormDefault="unqualified"
     elementFormDefault="qualified"
     xmlns:xs="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema"
     xmlns:as02="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/manifest"
     xmlns:atom="http://www.w3.org/2005/Atom"
     targetNamespace="http://www.quantel.com/qstack/rasotwo">
  <import namespace="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/manifest/" schemaLocation="AS-02Manifest.xsd"/>
  <xs:element name="Files">
    <xs:complexType>
      <xs:choice>
        <xs:element name="File" type="as02:FileType" minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"/> <!-- for full listings-->
        <xs:element name="FileSummary"  minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"> <!-- for summary listings-->
          <xs:element name="FileName" type="xs:string" minOccurs="1" maxOccurs="1"/> <!-- last part of path name -->
          <xs:element name="Path" type="xs:anyURI" minOccurs="1" maxOccurs="1"/> <!-- Q note: namespace issue in implementation -->
          <xs:element name="Role" type="as02:FileRole" minOccurs="1" maxOccurs="1"/>
          <xs:element name="FileID" type="as02:UUID" minOccits="1" maxOccurs="1"/> <!-- contraining to UUIDs only --> 
        </xs:element>
        <xs:element ref="atom:link" minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"/> <!-- for link only listings-->
      <xs:choice>
    </xs:complexType>
  </xs:element>
</xs:schema>

HTTP status code 404

The resource or one of its parent resources could not be found on this store.

post /bundle/{bundleID}/media

Create a new empty essence component in the bundle using the given Reg-XML file descriptor. The essence component file will be open an ready for extension.

The body of the POST shall contain a valid Reg-XML (SMPTE 2001-2) serialization of a class that is the extension of an AAF FileDescriptor class.

  • For video data, this will be an extension of PictureDescriptor.
  • For audio data, this will be a SoundDescriptor or one of its extensions.
  • For ancilliary data, such as captions, this will an extension of DataEssenceDescriptor.

Certain properties of the descriptor will be used by the AS-02 API to determine aspects of theessence component to be created, such as index type (clip or frame wrapped), index edit rate etc..

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

Query Parameters

  • id: (string - pattern: (urn:uuid:)?[0-9a-fA-f]{8}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{12})

    An unique identifier for a new resource provided prior to its creation. The service will either:

    • proceed to try to create a resource with the given identifier, or
    • respond with a bad request status.

    This is an optional parameter of type UUID. If no id is provided, the service will generate a type 4 pseudo-random UUID to identify the resource.

  • rushID: (string - pattern: (urn:uuid:)?[0-9a-fA-f]{8}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{12})

    Identifier of a source package to set at the end of the source reference chain. If not set, one will be auto-generated.

    The purpose of defining a source package at the end of the reference chain is to provide a common source identifier for essence components that:

    • provide partial representations of the same source material, possibly consisting of overlapping subclips;
    • provide different qualities of rendition of the same source material.
  • trackIndex: (integer)

    Non-negative integer number to identify the track (video) or group of tracks (audio) as essence component file names within the bundle, e.g. video0.mxf, audio3.mxf.

  • firstDecodeUnit: (integer)

    Index or decode time stamp (DTS) for the first expected access unit to be stored. As the access unit service can receive units out-of-order within a few playable seconds, it requires a starting window in which to expect the first unit.

  • origin: (integer)

    A value measured in edit units for the offset from zero of an item of content, used to define the relationship between the primary file package and the source package at the end of the source reference chain. THe value is a count of the number essence units missing after the zero point of the rush source material. More than one essence component for the same rushID can be stored in this or other bundles and each may have different extent.

  • offset: (integer)

    A slight nudge left or right required to align - often for reasons of lip sync.- related essence components. When creating a version file, one component, typically the video component, is nominated as the master component. The master component should have an offset value of zero, which is the default value for this query parameter. The audio component may have an offset value, measured in the sample rate of the audio, representing a slight offset that is required to synchronize the audio decoder with the video decoder. The opposite of MXF's Origin, this is a count of the number of missing samples that exist after the zero point. This will often be a negative value to ensure that the audio decoding can start prior to the presentation of the frame.

    Note that a timecode track in an audio essece component file is aligned with the origin, not with the offset.

  • startTimecode: (string - default: 00:00:00:00 - pattern: [0-2][0-9]:[0-5][0-9]:[0-5][0-9][:;][0-2][0-9](\.[01])?)

    Timecode value to set for the first access unit. This value is set to a default of the zero timecode (00:00:00:00 or 00:00:00;00) if no value is provided. The value is overridden if timecode if provided per access unit or range of access units.

    Note that for audio tracks where the timecode is video frame rate based, the origin is applied but an offset of 0 is set for the timecode track. The timecode value is as specified in SMPTE ST0258 Transfer of Edit Decision Lists, e.g. 01:02:03:04 for non-drop-frame and 01:02:03;04 for drop frame.

  • is90000Hz: (boolean)

    Set to true to indicate that the access units will be posted with decode and/or presentation timestamps measured as per MPEG-2 transport streams, at 90000Hz. The service should be able to cope with some jitter in this case. If access units are to be sent based on a continuous, index-based counter, set the value to its default of false.

  • samplesPerAccessUnit: (integer - default: 1 - minimum: 1)

    Number of samples per access unit as received, which is typically the default value of 1 for video. Other common values are 1024 for AAC audio and 192 for AES audio in a transport stream (SMPTE 0302). Note that this is not necessarily the value as stored in the MXF essence component, as in the case of AES audio is stored as clip-wrapped 48kHz PCM samples in MXF files.

    A known problem of this approach does not allow for variable numbers of samples per frame. To work with PCM audio at 30000/1001 or 60000/1001 frame rates, set to 8008 and compine PCM samples into five frame or ten frame groups.

Type: application/xml

HTTP status code 201

Details of the newly created AS-02 file, now present on the containing bundle's manifest file.

Headers

  • Location: (string)

    Full URL path to the newly created AS02 file, which includes the file ID.

Body

Type: application/xml

Schema:

<xs:schema attributeFormDefault="unqualified"
    elementFormDefault="qualified"
    xmlns:xs="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema"
    xmlns:as02="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/manifest"
    targetNamespace="http://www.quantel.com/qstack/rasotwo">
  <import namespace="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/manifest/" schemaLocation="AS-02Manifest.xsd"/>
  <xs:element name="File" type="as02:FileType" minOccurs="1" maxOccurs="1"/>
</xs:schema>

Problem creating the essence compomponent for reasons including:

  • Invalid query parameters;
  • Conflicts with existing identifiers;

/bundle/{bundleID}/media/{mediaID} get delete

Create, read, update, close and delete a specific essence component file.

get

Access manifest information about the essence component file.

delete

Delete the identified essence component file from the bundle.

get /bundle/{bundleID}/media/{mediaID}

Access manifest information about the essence component file.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

  • mediaID: required (string)

    Either the FileID or the part of the Path element after media/ is the file entry stored in the manifest file. The .mxf file extension part at the end of the path may be omitted.

HTTP status code 200

Details of the AS-02 file requested extracted from the containing bundle's manifest file.

Body

Type: application/xml

Schema:

<xs:schema attributeFormDefault="unqualified"
    elementFormDefault="qualified"
    xmlns:xs="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema"
    xmlns:as02="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/manifest"
    targetNamespace="http://www.quantel.com/qstack/rasotwo">
  <import namespace="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/manifest/" schemaLocation="AS-02Manifest.xsd"/>
  <xs:element name="File" type="as02:FileType" minOccurs="1" maxOccurs="1"/>
</xs:schema>

/bundle/{bundleID}/media/{mediaID}/aaf-xml get

Read the essence component file in XML format.

Note that writing in Reg-XML format is not supported.

get

Produces a MXF Reg-XML (SMPTE 2001-2) file as stored in the AS-02 bundle.

get /bundle/{bundleID}/media/{mediaID}/aaf-xml

Produces a MXF Reg-XML (SMPTE 2001-2) file as stored in the AS-02 bundle.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

  • mediaID: required (string)

    Either the FileID or the part of the Path element after media/ is the file entry stored in the manifest file. The .mxf file extension part at the end of the path may be omitted.

HTTP status code 200

Default MXF version file in XML format.

Body

Type: application/xml

Schema:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>

	<xs:include schemaLocation="fcd-st2001-1a-2013.xsd"/>
	<xs:import namespace="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" schemaLocation="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink.xsd"/>
	<xs:simpleType name="TargetType">
		<xs:union memberTypes="xs:token aaf:AUID aaf:PackageIDType">
			<xs:simpleType>
				<xs:restriction base="xs:string">
					<xs:pattern value="([^\s]+\s)?[^\s]+"/>
				</xs:restriction>
			</xs:simpleType>
		</xs:union>
	</xs:simpleType>
	<xs:simpleType name="ByteOrderType">
		<xs:restriction base="xs:string">
			<xs:enumeration value="BigEndian"/>
			<xs:enumeration value="LittleEndian"/>
		</xs:restriction>
	</xs:simpleType>
	<xs:simpleType name="HexByteArrayType">
		<xs:restriction base="xs:string">
			<xs:pattern value="(\s*[0-9a-fA-F][0-9a-fA-F])*\s*"/>
		</xs:restriction>
	</xs:simpleType>
	<xs:attribute name="uid" type="aaf:TargetType"/>

/bundle/{bundleID}/media/{mediaID}/aaf-xml/descriptor get

Read the AAF file descriptor from the picture, sound or data track of the primary package of the the MXF file in Reg-XML (SMPEG 2001-2) format. The file descriptor is in the same format as can be posted to create a new, empty essence component file.

get

Produces a MXF Reg-XML (SMPTE 2001-2) file descriptor from the picture, sound or data track of the primary package of the the MXF file.

get /bundle/{bundleID}/media/{mediaID}/aaf-xml/descriptor

Produces a MXF Reg-XML (SMPTE 2001-2) file descriptor from the picture, sound or data track of the primary package of the the MXF file.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

  • mediaID: required (string)

    Either the FileID or the part of the Path element after media/ is the file entry stored in the manifest file. The .mxf file extension part at the end of the path may be omitted.

HTTP status code 200

File descriptor in XML format.

Type: application/xml

/bundle/{bundleID}/media/{mediaID}/stream get put

Read or write an MXF file in its native KLV format.

get

Reads the default version file as an MXF file as stored in the AS-02 bundle.

put

Create or replace the MXF file by providing a complete KLV-encoded version.

get /bundle/{bundleID}/media/{mediaID}/stream

Reads the default version file as an MXF file as stored in the AS-02 bundle.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

  • mediaID: required (string)

    Either the FileID or the part of the Path element after media/ is the file entry stored in the manifest file. The .mxf file extension part at the end of the path may be omitted.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Type: application/mxf

/bundle/{bundleID}/media/{mediaID}/close post

Initiate the process of closing the essence component file. An essence component file may be in one of three states according to this API:

open

Accepting new access units and not in a closed complete state on the underlying store.

closing

Not accepting new access units and may or may not be in a closed complete state on the underlying store.

closed

Not accepting new access units and in a closed complete state on the underlying store.

post

Start the process of closing the essence component file and stop accepting new access units.

post /bundle/{bundleID}/media/{mediaID}/close

Start the process of closing the essence component file and stop accepting new access units.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

  • mediaID: required (string)

    Either the FileID or the part of the Path element after media/ is the file entry stored in the manifest file. The .mxf file extension part at the end of the path may be omitted.

HTTP status code 204

Process of closing the essence component file has started. Check media information via '../accessUnit' resource for current state.

HTTP status code 404

The resource or one of its parent resources could not be found on this store.

Body

Type: application/xml

Schema:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>

you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.

Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software 
distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS, 
WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.

/bundle/{bundleID}/media/{mediaID}/accessUnit get

Provides summary information about an essence component file, including whether the file is still open for writing and the current duration available for reading through this API.

get

Request media information about the essence component.

get /bundle/{bundleID}/media/{mediaID}/accessUnit

Request media information about the essence component.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

  • mediaID: required (string)

    Either the FileID or the part of the Path element after media/ is the file entry stored in the manifest file. The .mxf file extension part at the end of the path may be omitted.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Type: application/json

Schema:

{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema#",
  "id": "http://amwa.tv/as-02api",
  "description": "Summary information about the current state of an essence component file as accessible through the API.",
  "type": "object",
  "properties": { 
    "LastPartition": {
      "id": "http://amwa.tv/as-02api/LastPartition",
      "type": "integer",
      "description": "Inclusive index of the last partition in the essence component file.",
      "minimum": 0,
      "exclusiveMinimum": false
    },
    "FileClosed": {
      "id": "http://amwa.tv/as-02api/FileClosed",
      "type": "string",
      "description": "Status of the essence component file, as to whether it is: 'open' - accepting new access units; 'closing' - not accepting new access units but file may not yet be closed and complete; 'closed' - not accepting access units and file is closed and complete on the store.",
      "enum": [
        "open",
        "closing",
        "closed"
      ]
    },
    "EditRate": {
      "id": "http://amwa.tv/as-02api/EditRate",
      "type": "string",
      "description": "Edit rate for the essence as a rational value in format <numerator>/<denominator>, e.g. 60000/1001.",
      "default": "25/1",
      "pattern": "\\d+/\\d+"
    },
    "Duration": {
      "id": "http://amwa.tv/as-02api/Duration",
      "type": "integer",
      "description": "Count of the total number of edit units accessible from the essence component file.",
      "minimum": 0,
      "exclusiveMinimum": false
    },
    "AccessUnitType": {
      "id": "http://amwa.tv/as-02api/AccessUnitType",
      "type": "string",
      "description": "Indication of the type of essence contained in the file. Full information should be retrieved from the MXF file descriptor available through the '/descriptor', '/stream' and '/aaf-xml' sub-resources.",
      "minLength": 1,
      "default": "Frame",
      "enum": [
        "unknown", "aac", "iframeonly", "longgop", "sample", "smpte302m", "ancdata"
      ]
    }
  },
  "required": [
    "LastPartition",
    "FileClosed",
    "EditRate",
    "Duration",
    "AccessUnitType"
  ]
}

Example:

{
  "LastPartition": 3,
  "FileClosed": "closing",
  "EditRate": "60000/10",
  "Duration": 1234,
  "AccessUnitType": "iframeonly"
}

  "id": "http://amwa.tv/as-02api",
  "description": "Summary information about the current state of an essence component file as accessible through the API.",
  "type": "object",
  "properties": { 
    "LastPartition": {
      "id": "http://amwa.tv/as-02api/LastPartition",
      "type": "integer",
      "description": "Inclusive index of the last partition in the essence component file.",
      "minimum": 0,
      "exclusiveMinimum": false
    },
    "FileClosed": {
      "id": "http://amwa.tv/as-02api/FileClosed",
      "type": "string",
      "description": "Status of the essence component file, as to whether it is: 'open' - accepting new access units; 'closing' - not accepting new access units but file may not yet be closed and complete; 'closed' - not accepting access units and file is closed and complete on the store.",
      "enum": [
        "open",
        "closing",
        "closed"
      ]
    },
    "EditRate": {
      "id": "http://amwa.tv/as-02api/EditRate",
      "type": "string",
      "description": "Edit rate for the essence as a rational value in format <numerator>/<denominator>, e.g. 60000/1001.",
      "default": "25/1",
      "pattern": "\\d+/\\d+"
    },
    "Duration": {
      "id": "http://amwa.tv/as-02api/Duration",
      "type": "integer",
      "description": "Count of the total number of edit units accessible from the essence component file.",
      "minimum": 0,
      "exclusiveMinimum": false
    },
    "AccessUnitType": {
      "id": "http://amwa.tv/as-02api/AccessUnitType",
      "type": "string",
      "description": "Indication of the type of essence contained in the file. Full information should be retrieved from the MXF file descriptor available through the '/descriptor', '/stream' and '/aaf-xml' sub-resources.",
      "minLength": 1,
      "default": "Frame",
      "enum": [
        "unknown", "aac", "iframeonly", "longgop", "sample", "smpte302m", "ancdata"
      ]
    }
  },
  "required": [
    "LastPartition",
    "FileClosed",
    "EditRate",
    "Duration",
    "AccessUnitType"
  ]
}

Example:

{
  "LastPartition": 3,
  "FileClosed": "closing",
  "EditRate": "60000/10",
  "Duration": 1234,
  "AccessUnitType": "iframeonly"
}

/bundle/{bundleID}/media/{mediaID}/partition/{range} get

Read complete MXF partitions from the essence component file in their native KLV format. Index units are whole partitions, starting with 0 for the header partition. Timecode and offset position ranges are not supported.

get

get /bundle/{bundleID}/media/{mediaID}/partition/{range}

  • Request

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

  • mediaID: required (string)

    Either the FileID or the part of the Path element after media/ is the file entry stored in the manifest file. The .mxf file extension part at the end of the path may be omitted.

  • : ()

/bundle/{bundleID}/version get post

Create, list, read and replace and delete all version files stored in the AS-02 bundle.

get

List details of all version files in the bundle.

post

Create a new version file that automatically updates as the related open essence component files are growing.

get /bundle/{bundleID}/version

List details of all version files in the bundle.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

Query Parameters

  • skip: (integer)

    Number of pages of version items to skip (hide) before starting to display values.

  • limit: (integer - default: 20)

    Limit of the mixumum number of version items to include on each page.

  • detail: (one of full, summary, link - default: full)

    Amount of detail to return for each version items in the collection, where:

    • full: Complete manifest details for each item.
    • summary: Some useful details about each bundle, including its name, identifier, creator and number of files.
    • link: A list of identifiers for bundles.

HTTP status code 200

Successful retrieval of a list of file details.

Body

Type: application/xml

Schema:

<xs:schema attributeFormDefault="unqualified"
     elementFormDefault="qualified"
     xmlns:xs="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema"
     xmlns:as02="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/manifest"
     xmlns:atom="http://www.w3.org/2005/Atom"
     targetNamespace="http://www.quantel.com/qstack/rasotwo">
  <import namespace="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/manifest/" schemaLocation="AS-02Manifest.xsd"/>
  <xs:element name="Files">
    <xs:complexType>
      <xs:choice>
        <xs:element name="File" type="as02:FileType" minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"/> <!-- for full listings-->
        <xs:element name="FileSummary"  minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"> <!-- for summary listings-->
          <xs:element name="FileName" type="xs:string" minOccurs="1" maxOccurs="1"/> <!-- last part of path name -->
          <xs:element name="Path" type="xs:anyURI" minOccurs="1" maxOccurs="1"/> <!-- Q note: namespace issue in implementation -->
          <xs:element name="Role" type="as02:FileRole" minOccurs="1" maxOccurs="1"/>
          <xs:element name="FileID" type="as02:UUID" minOccits="1" maxOccurs="1"/> <!-- contraining to UUIDs only --> 
        </xs:element>
        <xs:element ref="atom:link" minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"/> <!-- for link only listings-->
      <xs:choice>
    </xs:complexType>
  </xs:element>
</xs:schema>

post /bundle/{bundleID}/version

Create a new version file that automatically updates as the related open essence component files are growing.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

Query Parameters

  • id: (string - pattern: (urn:uuid:)?[0-9a-fA-f]{8}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{12})

    An unique identifier for a new resource provided prior to its creation. The service will either:

    • proceed to try to create a resource with the given identifier, or
    • respond with a bad request status.

    This is an optional parameter of type UUID. If no id is provided, the service will generate a type 4 pseudo-random UUID to identify the resource.

  • name: (string)

    Name for the version file. Should be a string that is suitable for use as a file name.

    Omitting the name is equivalent to setting it to the name of the bundle's folder with .mxf appended, thereby creating the bundle's default version file.

  • master: required (string - pattern: (urn:uuid:)?[0-9a-fA-f]{8}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{12})

    UUID for the master essence component file in the bundle. This value must be provided and must be the identifier for the essence component file, not the rush identifier referenced from within the file.

    The master essence component file within a version is the one that provides the overall edit rate for the version file and contains the timecode track that will be used as the output timecode track for the version file.

  • component: (string - repeat: true - pattern: (urn:uuid:)?[0-9a-fA-f]{8}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{4}-[0-9a-fA-F]{12})

    Zero or more essence component files that are synchronous with the master component and being recorded at the same time as part of this version. The master essence component file should not be repeated here. If only a single master essence component file exists for the version file, there is no need to list it here.

HTTP status code 201

Details of the newly created AS-02 file, now present on the containing bundle's manifest file.

Headers

  • Location: (string)

    Full URL path to the newly created AS02 file, which includes the file ID.

Body

Type: application/xml

Schema:

<xs:schema attributeFormDefault="unqualified"
    elementFormDefault="qualified"
    xmlns:xs="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema"
    xmlns:as02="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/manifest"
    targetNamespace="http://www.quantel.com/qstack/rasotwo">
  <import namespace="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/manifest/" schemaLocation="AS-02Manifest.xsd"/>
  <xs:element name="File" type="as02:FileType" minOccurs="1" maxOccurs="1"/>
</xs:schema>

HTTP status code 400

Problem creating the version file for reasons including:

  • Invalid query parameters;
  • Conflicts with existing identifiers;
  • Master essence component file included as a component.

Body

Type: application/xml

Schema:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>

 <xs:schema attributeFormDefault="unqualified"
     elementFormDefault="qualified"

/bundle/{bundleID}/version/{versionID} get delete

Access manifest information about the identified version file.

get

Retrieve details about the identified version file from the containing bundle's manifest file.

delete

Delete the identified version file from the bundle.

get /bundle/{bundleID}/version/{versionID}

Retrieve details about the identified version file from the containing bundle's manifest file.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

  • versionID: required (string)

    Either the FileID or the Path of the file as stored in the manifest file. The .mxf part of the path may be omitted.

HTTP status code 200

Details of the AS-02 file requested extracted from the containing bundle's manifest file.

/bundle/{bundleID}/version/{versionID}/aaf-xml get

Read the version file in XML format.

Note that writing in Reg-XML format is not supported.

get

Produces a MXF Reg-XML (SMPTE 2001-2) file as stored in the AS-02 bundle.

get /bundle/{bundleID}/version/{versionID}/aaf-xml

Produces a MXF Reg-XML (SMPTE 2001-2) file as stored in the AS-02 bundle.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

  • versionID: required (string)

    Either the FileID or the Path of the file as stored in the manifest file. The .mxf part of the path may be omitted.

HTTP status code 200

Default MXF version file in XML format.

/bundle/{bundleID}/version/{versionID}/stream get put

Read or write an MXF file in its native KLV format.

get

Reads the default version file as an MXF file as stored in the AS-02 bundle.

put

Create or replace the MXF file by providing a complete KLV-encoded version.

get /bundle/{bundleID}/version/{versionID}/stream

Reads the default version file as an MXF file as stored in the AS-02 bundle.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

  • versionID: required (string)

    Either the FileID or the Path of the file as stored in the manifest file. The .mxf part of the path may be omitted.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Type: application/mxf

/bundle/{bundleID}/version/default/aaf-xml get

Read the default version file in XML format.

Note that writing in Reg-XML format is not supported.

get

Produces a MXF Reg-XML (SMPTE 2001-2) file as stored in the AS-02 bundle.

get /bundle/{bundleID}/version/default/aaf-xml

Produces a MXF Reg-XML (SMPTE 2001-2) file as stored in the AS-02 bundle.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

/bundle/{bundleID}/version/default/stream get put

Read or write default version file in its native KLV format.

get

Reads the default version file as an MXF file as stored in the AS-02 bundle.

put

Create or replace the MXF file by providing a complete KLV-encoded version.

get /bundle/{bundleID}/version/default/stream

Reads the default version file as an MXF file as stored in the AS-02 bundle.

  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

/bundle/{bundleID}/extra get

Access to create, reasd, update and delete vendor-specific sub-folders of the AS-02 bundle's extra folder.

get

Retrieve a list of all vendor sub-folders in the extra folder.

get /bundle/{bundleID}/extra

Retrieve a list of all vendor sub-folders in the extra folder.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

Query Parameters

  • skip: (integer)

    Number of pages of extra items to skip (hide) before starting to display values.

  • limit: (integer - default: 20)

    Limit of the mixumum number of extra items to include on each page.

  • detail: (one of full, summary, link - default: full)

    Amount of detail to return for each extra items in the collection, where:

    • full: Complete manifest details for each item.
    • summary: Some useful details about each bundle, including its name, identifier, creator and number of files.
    • link: A list of identifiers for bundles.

HTTP status code 200

Successful retrieval of a list of file details.

Body

Type: application/xml

Schema:

<xs:schema attributeFormDefault="unqualified"
     elementFormDefault="qualified"
     xmlns:xs="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema"
     xmlns:as02="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/manifest"
     xmlns:atom="http://www.w3.org/2005/Atom"
     targetNamespace="http://www.quantel.com/qstack/rasotwo">
  <import namespace="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/manifest/" schemaLocation="AS-02Manifest.xsd"/>
  <xs:element name="Files">
    <xs:complexType>
      <xs:choice>
        <xs:element name="File" type="as02:FileType" minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"/> <!-- for full listings-->
        <xs:element name="FileSummary"  minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"> <!-- for summary listings-->
          <xs:element name="FileName" type="xs:string" minOccurs="1" maxOccurs="1"/> <!-- last part of path name -->
          <xs:element name="Path" type="xs:anyURI" minOccurs="1" maxOccurs="1"/> <!-- Q note: namespace issue in implementation -->
          <xs:element name="Role" type="as02:FileRole" minOccurs="1" maxOccurs="1"/>
          <xs:element name="FileID" type="as02:UUID" minOccits="1" maxOccurs="1"/> <!-- contraining to UUIDs only --> 
        </xs:element>
        <xs:element ref="atom:link" minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"/> <!-- for link only listings-->
      <xs:choice>
    </xs:complexType>
  </xs:element>
</xs:schema>

HTTP status code 404

The resource or one of its parent resources could not be found on this store.

Body

Type: application/xml

Schema:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
  
<!--

/bundle/{bundleID}/extra/{vendorName} get post delete

Represents a specific vendor subfolder called vendorName within the AS-02 bundle.

get

Read details of all files in the folder with Path set to extra/{vendorName} in the comntaining bundle manifest file.

post
delete

get /bundle/{bundleID}/extra/{vendorName}

Read details of all files in the folder with Path set to extra/{vendorName} in the comntaining bundle manifest file.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

  • vendorName: required (string)

    Name of a vendor-specific sub-folder inside the AS-02 bundle extra folder. By concention, this is a the same as the domain name of the company.

    As RAML does not support dynamic nested resource paths, access to vendor sub-paths is limited to a depth of 3 subfolders.

    Example:

    quantel.com

Query Parameters

  • skip: (integer)

    Number of pages of extra items to skip (hide) before starting to display values.

  • limit: (integer - default: 20)

    Limit of the mixumum number of extra items to include on each page.

  • detail: (one of full, summary, link - default: full)

    Amount of detail to return for each extra items in the collection, where:

    • full: Complete manifest details for each item.
    • summary: Some useful details about each bundle, including its name, identifier, creator and number of files.
    • link: A list of identifiers for bundles.

HTTP status code 200

Successful retrieval of a list of file details.

Body

Type: application/xml

Schema:

     elementFormDefault="qualified"

post /bundle/{bundleID}/extra/{vendorName}

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

  • vendorName: required (string)

    Name of a vendor-specific sub-folder inside the AS-02 bundle extra folder. By concention, this is a the same as the domain name of the company.

    As RAML does not support dynamic nested resource paths, access to vendor sub-paths is limited to a depth of 3 subfolders.

    Example:

    quantel.com

/bundle/{bundleID}/shim.xml get put post

Create, read or update the AS-02 shim file stored for the bundle.

get

Read the AS-02 shim file stored for this bundle.

put

Create or replace the AS-02 shim file stored for this bundle.

post

Create or replace the existing AS-02 shim file using query parameters.

get /bundle/{bundleID}/shim.xml

Read the AS-02 shim file stored for this bundle.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Type: application/xml

Schema:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<xs:schema xmlns:xs="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema"
    xmlns:shim="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/shim"
    targetNamespace="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/shim"
    elementFormDefault="qualified"
    attributeFormDefault="unqualified">
    <!-- ShimType -->
    <xs:complexType name="ShimType">
        <xs:sequence>
            <xs:element name="ShimName" type="xs:string"/>
            <xs:element name="ShimID" type="xs:anyURI" minOccurs="0"/>
            <xs:element name="AnnotationText" type="xs:string" minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"/>
			<xs:element name="ApplicationSpec" type="xs:string" minOccurs="0"/>
        </xs:sequence>
        <xs:anyAttribute namespace="##other" processContents="lax"/>
    </xs:complexType>
    <xs:element name="Shim" type="shim:ShimType"/>
</xs:schema>

post /bundle/{bundleID}/shim.xml

Create or replace the existing AS-02 shim file using query parameters.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • bundleID: required (string)

    Either a bundle name that matches the BundleName element in a bundle manifest file or a UUID bundle identifier matching the BundleID property.

Query Parameters

  • name: (string - default: QStack rasotwo default shim)

    Human-readable identifier for the shim.

  • ID: (string - default: http://amwa.tv/as-02/as-02/defaultShim)

    URI for the shim, which should be a resovable reference to an external document that defines the shim. Should be a valid URI but does not need to be resovable at the time of the request.

  • annotation: (string - repeat: true)

    Set of descriptions for the shim.

HTTP status code 201

The newly created or replaced shim file for the bundle.

Body

Type: application/xml

Schema:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<xs:schema xmlns:xs="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema"
    xmlns:shim="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/shim"
    targetNamespace="http://www.amwa.tv/as-02/1.0/shim"
    elementFormDefault="qualified"
    attributeFormDefault="unqualified">
    <!-- ShimType -->
    <xs:complexType name="ShimType">
        <xs:sequence>
            <xs:element name="ShimName" type="xs:string"/>
            <xs:element name="ShimID" type="xs:anyURI" minOccurs="0"/>
            <xs:element name="AnnotationText" type="xs:string" minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"/>
			<xs:element name="ApplicationSpec" type="xs:string" minOccurs="0"/>
        </xs:sequence>
        <xs:anyAttribute namespace="##other" processContents="lax"/>
    </xs:complexType>
    <xs:element name="Shim" type="shim:ShimType"/>
</xs:schema>

HTTP status code 400

Service Status

Provided status information about the health of the service, including whether the service can access other services that it is dependent on, such as file systems, databases or search engines.

/ping get

get

get /ping

  • Response

HTTP status code 200

The service is operating normally and cannot detect any issues.

HTTP status code 500

A system-level problem is precenting the service from operating as normal.

HTTP status code 502

A problem has been detected accessing a dependent service, such as a database or search engine.

  • Bundle Collection
  • Service Status
